9*(B^4*l + B^3*l^2)/(B^5*l^4 + B^7 + 2*B^4*l^3 + 4*B^4*l + 5*B^3*l^2 + 2*B^2*l^3 + B*l^2)) + (B^5*l^5 + B^5*l^3 + 3*B^4*l^4 + B^4*l^2 + 2*B^3*l^3)/(B^5*l^5 + B^7*l + B^6*l^2 + B^5*l^3 + 3*B^4*l^4 + 3*B^4*l^2 + 5*B^3*l^3 + B^2*l^4) <= (B^5*l^4 + 2*B^4*l^3 + B^4*l + 3*B^3*l^2 + B^2*l^3)/(B^5*l^4 + B^7 + 2*B^4*l^3 + 4*B^4*l + 5*B^3*l^2 + 2*B^2*l^3 + B*l^2)
